Caption: Growing a new fungus is always interesting. This is Cordyceps militaris #cordycepsmilitaris a fungi that until recently was not allowed to be grown here in Australia. Now we can legally grow this, I was curious to give it a go - especially after investing so much time into trying to grow Cordyceps gunnii, unsuccessfully! Not my best grow! And I have been watching lots of US growers really get to dial these in to be an art. But I grew these on white rice with no nutrients to start out so I could get an idea of growth, yield, and other characteristics that may help later! One big hint, don't try to grow these when it is hot without cooling! #guerrillamycology #fungiculture #ğŸ„ #fungi #fungus #funghi #hongos #myceliumrunning #radicalmycology #radmycology #thinkfungi #mycology #mycophile #mycophilia #mycelium #mushrooms #myceliumrunning #myceliumnetwork #myceliummood #cordyceps #cordycepsmilitaris #cordycepsgunnii #introducedfungi #notnativefungi #notwildfungi #ethnomycology #entheogenicfungi #fungiphotography #mushroomphotography

Many Indigenous cultures that have deeply rooted ethnomycological history, especially those of the northern hemisphere in Scandinavia and Siberia, claim that fruitings of ground-dwelling, fleshy macrofungi occur in greater abundance on the full moon. Since the moons gravity pulls the terrestrial tides (ground water) further up to the surface of the soil on full moons and even more so on new moons, it would make sense that lunar events have a direct effect on fruiting of certain species.
